-- =============================================
-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 08/03/2022
-- Description:	To add user account
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_AddUser] 
	@I_UserId VARCHAR(50),
	@I_Role INT,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_ErrTxt VARCHAR(250) OUTPUT
	
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @V_UserCount INT

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'AddUser'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @V_UserCount = 0
	SET @O_ErrTxt = ''

		BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		
		SELECT @V_UserCount = COUNT(UserId) FROM TBL_DTS_USER
		WHERE UserId = @I_UserId 

		IF (@V_UserCount > 0)
		BEGIN
			SET @O_Success = 1
			SET @O_ErrTxt = 'User already existed!'
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN

		INSERT INTO TBL_DTS_USER
		(UserId, RoleId, Password, Active)
		VALUES
		(@I_UserId, @I_Role, 'Passw0rd', 1)

		END

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		SET @O_ErrTxt = @ERR_MSG
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_BatchUpdateDeviceInfo]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author:		Jackson
-- Create date: 06/05/2021
-- Version:		1.0.0.0
-- Description:	To batch update the device info
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_BatchUpdateDeviceInfo] 
	@I_tblBUDeviceInfo dbo.TDTS_DTS_DEVICE READONLY,
	@I_LotNumber VARCHAR(100),
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_SourceSubstrateId VARCHAR(100),
	@I_TargetSubstrateId VARCHAR(100),
	@I_BinResult VARCHAR(100),
	@I_BinCode VARCHAR(100),
	@I_BinDesc VARCHAR(100),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @BinResultName VARCHAR(50)
	
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'BatchUpdateDevice'
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

			SELECT * INTO #TMPBUDeviceInfo FROM @I_tblBUDeviceInfo

			SELECT @BinResultName = BinResultName FROM TBL_DTS_CONFIG_BINRESULT
			WHERE BinResultId = @I_BinResult

			UPDATE dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
			SET 
			SourceSubstrateId = CASE WHEN @I_SourceSubstrateId IS NOT NULL THEN @I_SourceSubstrateId ELSE SourceSubstrateId END,
			TargetSubstrateId = CASE WHEN @I_TargetSubstrateId IS NOT NULL THEN @I_TargetSubstrateId ELSE TargetSubstrateId END,
			BinResult = CASE WHEN @BinResultName != '' THEN @BinResultName ELSE BinResult END,
			BinCode = CASE WHEN @I_BinCode IS NOT NULL THEN @I_BinCode ELSE BinCode END,
			BinDesc = CASE WHEN @I_BinDesc IS NOT NULL THEN @I_BinDesc ELSE BinDesc END
			FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS 
			INNER JOIN #TMPBUDeviceInfo DI ON  DI.DeviceId = DTS.DeviceId
			WHERE DTS.LotNumber = @I_LotNumber and DTS.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId

			--UPDATE dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
			--SET 
			--SourceSubstrateId = CASE WHEN LEN(ISNULL(@I_SourceSubstrateId, '')) = 0 THEN SourceSubstrateId ELSE @I_SourceSubstrateId END,
			--TargetSubstrateId = CASE WHEN LEN(ISNULL(@I_TargetSubstrateId, '')) = 0 THEN TargetSubstrateId ELSE @I_TargetSubstrateId END,
			--BinResult = CASE WHEN LEN(ISNULL(@I_BinResult, '')) = 0 THEN BinResult ELSE @I_BinResult END,
			--BinCode = CASE WHEN LEN(ISNULL(@I_BinCode, '')) = 0 THEN BinCode ELSE @I_BinCode END,
			--BinDesc = CASE WHEN LEN(ISNULL(@I_BinDesc, '')) = 0 THEN BinDesc ELSE @I_BinDesc END
			--FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS 
			--INNER JOIN #TMPBUDeviceInfo DI ON  DI.DeviceId = DTS.DeviceId
			--WHERE DTS.LotNumber = @I_LotNumber and DTS.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId

			DROP TABLE #TMPBUDeviceInfo
			
		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 08/03/2022
-- Description:	Change password
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_ChangePassword]
	@I_UserId VARCHAR(50),
	@I_OldPassword VARCHAR(250),
	@I_NewPassword VARCHAR(250),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_ErrTxt VARCHAR(250) OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @V_UserCount INT, @V_PassMatchCount INT

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'ChangePassword'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @V_UserCount = 0
	SET @O_ErrTxt = ''
	SET @V_PassMatchCount = 0

		BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		
		SELECT @V_UserCount = COUNT(UserId) FROM TBL_DTS_USER
		WHERE UserId = @I_UserId and Active = 1

		SELECT @V_PassMatchCount = COUNT(UserId) FROM TBL_DTS_USER
		WHERE UserId = @I_UserId and Password = @I_OldPassword and Active = 1

		IF (@V_UserCount = 0)
			BEGIN

				SET @O_Success = 1
				SET @O_ErrTxt = 'User not found!'

			END
		ELSE IF (@V_PassMatchCount = 0)
			BEGIN

				SET @O_Success = 2
				SET @O_ErrTxt = 'Password not match!'

			END
		ELSE
			BEGIN

			UPDATE TBL_DTS_USER
			SET
			Password = @I_NewPassword
			WHERE UserId = @I_UserId AND Password = @I_OldPassword AND Active = 1

			END

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		SET @O_ErrTxt = @ERR_MSG
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_CopyScannedDeviceInfo]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 03/09/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Copy and delete TEMP table data to LOG_SCANDEVICEINFO table
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_CopyScannedDeviceInfo]
		@I_LotInfoId VARCHAR(50),
		@O_Success INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @CurrDateTime DATETIME

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'CopyTempDataToLogTable'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @CurrDateTime = GETDATE()

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

		INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_SCANDEVICEINFO
		(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ScanDateTime, ValidateScannedResult)
		SELECT tp.LotInfoId, tp.DeviceId, tp.BinResult, tp.BinCode, tp.BinDesc, tp.Operation, @CurrDateTime, tp.ValidateResult
		FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO tp
		WHERE tp.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId

		DELETE FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson Chang
-- Create date	: 22/03/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description:	Storing lot information for DTS
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson Chang
-- Create date	: 01/09/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add in ValidateQuantity	
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_CreateBatchInfo] 

	@I_LotNumber			VARCHAR(50),
	@I_Operation			VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@I_LotQty1				INT  = NULL,
	@I_UserId				VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@I_ValidateQuantity		INT = NULL,
	@O_Success				INT = NULL OUTPUT,
	@O_LotInfoId			BIGINT = NULL OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'CreateBatchInfo'
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

			INSERT	INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO 
						(LotNumber, Operation, UserId, LotQty1, ValidateQuantity)
			Values (@I_LotNumber, @I_Operation, @I_UserId, @I_LotQty1, @I_ValidateQuantity)

			SELECT @O_LotInfoId = IDENT_CURRENT('dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO')

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_DeleteUser]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 08/03/2022
-- Description:	To delete user
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_DeleteUser] 
	@Tbl_UserList TDTS_DTS_UserId READONLY,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_ErrTxt VARCHAR(250) OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @V_UserCount INT

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'DeleteUser'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @V_UserCount = 0
	SET @O_ErrTxt = ''

		BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		
		SELECT * INTO TMPUserList FROM @Tbl_UserList

		SELECT @V_UserCount = COUNT(u.UserId) FROM TBL_DTS_USER u
		INNER JOIN TMPUserList tmp ON tmp.UserId = u.UserId
		WHERE u.UserId = tmp.UserId

		IF (@V_UserCount = 0)
		BEGIN
			SET @O_Success = 1
			SET @O_ErrTxt = 'User not found'
		END
		ELSE 
		BEGIN
			DELETE
			FROM TBL_DTS_User
			WHERE UserId in (SELECT * FROM TMPUserList)
		END

		DROP TABLE TMPUserList

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		SET @O_ErrTxt = @ERR_MSG
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAllDevice]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 28/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Get All Device Info
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 11/10/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add condition for Merge Lot to get all the device information that bin result not PREV FAILED
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAllDevice] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT = NULL,
	@I_LotNumber VARCHAR(100) = NULL,
	@I_TransactionType VARCHAR(50),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

	SET @O_Success = 0

	IF (@I_TransactionType = 'MergeLot')
		BEGIN
			SELECT t.LotInfoId, t.DeviceId, t.AliasId, t.SourceSubstrateId, t.TargetSubstrateId, t.SourcePositionId,
			t.TargetPositionId, t.FromX, t.FromY, t.ToX, t.ToY, b.BinResultId as BinResultId, t.BinCode, t.BinDesc, t.LotNumber, t.Pick 
			FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS t
			inner join TBL_DTS_CONFIG_BINRESULT b on b.BinResultName = t.BinResult
			WHERE t.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND t.LotNumber = @I_LotNumber AND b.BinResultName != 'PREV FAILED'
		END
	ELSE
		BEGIN
			SELECT t.LotInfoId, t.DeviceId, t.AliasId, t.SourceSubstrateId, t.TargetSubstrateId, t.SourcePositionId,
			t.TargetPositionId, t.FromX, t.FromY, t.ToX, t.ToY, b.BinResultId as BinResultId, t.BinCode, t.BinDesc, t.LotNumber, t.Pick 
			FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS t
			inner join TBL_DTS_CONFIG_BINRESULT b on b.BinResultName = t.BinResult
			WHERE t.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND t.LotNumber = @I_LotNumber
		END

	RETURN  @O_Success

END
GO

	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT = NULL,
	@I_LotNumber VARCHAR(100) = NULL,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

	SET @O_Success = 0

	SELECT t.LotInfoId, t.DeviceId, t.AliasId, t.SourceSubstrateId, t.TargetSubstrateId, t.SourcePositionId,
	t.TargetPositionId, t.FromX, t.FromY, t.ToX, t.ToY, b.BinResultId as BinResultId, t.BinCode, t.BinDesc, t.LotNumber, t.Pick

	RETURN  @O_Success

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAllDeviceDTS]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 28/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Get All Device Info
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 06/09/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add transaction type to get the device list that exclude the PREV FAILED record
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAllDeviceDTS] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT = NULL,
	@I_LotNumber VARCHAR(100) = NULL,
	@I_TransactionType VARCHAR(50),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

	SET @O_Success = 0

	IF (@I_TransactionType = 'SplitStandard' OR @I_TransactionType = 'SplitNonStandard' OR @I_TransactionType = 'SplitORT')
		BEGIN
			SELECT * FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and LotNumber = @I_LotNumber and BinResult != 'PREV FAILED' 
		END
	ELSE
		BEGIN
			SELECT LotInfoId, DeviceId, AliasId, SourceSubstrateId, TargetSubstrateId,
			SourcePositionId, TargetPositionId, FromX, FromY, ToX, ToY,
			BinResult = CASE WHEN BinResult = 'PREV FAILED' THEN 'UNKNOWN' ELSE BinResult END,
			BinCode, SAPBarcode, BinDesc, LotNumber, Pick
			FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and LotNumber = @I_LotNumber
		END

	RETURN  @O_Success

END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAllDeviceDTS_bkp20211015] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT = NULL,
	@I_LotNumber VARCHAR(100) = NULL,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN

	SET @O_Success = 0

	SELECT * FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
	WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and LotNumber = @I_LotNumber

	RETURN  @O_Success

END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAuditLog]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 23/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Get Audit Log
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 11/08/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add in additional child lot number for merge lot log and validate lot log
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAuditLog]

	@I_StartDateTime VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@I_EndDateTime VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)

	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
	
		SELECT a.UserId, b.EventName, a.EventDateTime, 
		(CASE WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NULL THEN m.MotherLotId
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NULL THEN s.MotherLotNumber
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NULL THEN u.UpdateLotNumber
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NOT NULL THEN 
			  (SELECT l.LotNumber from  TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT v 
			  inner join TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO l on l.LotInfoId = v.LotInfoId
			  where v.VlogId = a.ValidateLotId)
			  ELSE '' END) as MotherLotNumber,
		(CASE WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL THEN 
			(CASE WHEN m.ChildLotId2 IS NOT NULL AND m.ChildLotId3 IS NOT NULL AND m.ChildLotId4 IS NOT NULL THEN CONCAT(m.ChildLotId,' ', m.ChildLotId2,' ', m.ChildLotId3,' ', m.ChildLotId4)
				WHEN m.ChildLotId2 IS NOT NULL AND m.ChildLotId3 IS NOT NULL AND m.ChildLotId4 IS NULL THEN CONCAT(m.ChildLotId,' ', m.ChildLotId2,' ', m.ChildLotId3)
				WHEN m.ChildLotId2 IS NOT NULL AND m.ChildLotId3 IS NULL AND m.ChildLotId4 IS NULL THEN CONCAT(m.ChildLotId,' ', m.ChildLotId2) ELSE m.ChildLotId END)
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NOT NULL THEN s.ChildLotNumber
			  ELSE '' END) as ChildLotNumber,
		(CASE WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NULL THEN m.Operation
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NULL THEN s.Operation
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NULL THEN u.Operation
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL AND a.ValidateLotId IS NOT NULL THEN v.Operation
			  ELSE '' END) as Operation
		FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT a
		INNER JOIN TBL_DTS_CONFIG_EVENT b ON b.EventId = a.EventId
		LEFT JOIN TBL_DTS_LOG_MERGELOT m ON m.MergeLotId = a.MergeLotId
		LEFT JOIN TBL_DTS_LOG_SPLITLOT s ON s.SplitLotId = a.SplitLotId
		LEFT JOIN TBL_DTS_LOG_UPDATELOT u ON u.ULogId = a.UpdateLotId
		LEFT JOIN TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT v ON v.VLogId = a.ValidateLotId
		WHERE EventDateTime between @I_StartDateTime and @I_EndDateTime

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAuditLog_bkp20211015]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 23/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Get Audit Log
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetAuditLog_bkp20211015]

	@I_StartDateTime VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@I_EndDateTime VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)

	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
	
		SELECT a.UserId, b.EventName, a.EventDateTime, 
		(CASE WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL THEN m.MotherLotId
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL THEN s.MotherLotNumber
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NOT NULL THEN u.UpdateLotNumber
			  ELSE '' END) as MotherLotNumber,
		(CASE WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL THEN m.ChildLotId
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NOT NULL THEN s.ChildLotNumber
			  ELSE '' END) as ChildLotNumber,
		(CASE WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL THEN m.Operation
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NOT NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NULL THEN s.Operation
			  WHEN a.MergeLotId IS NULL AND a.SplitLotId IS NULL AND a.UpdateLotId IS NOT NULL THEN u.Operation
			  ELSE '' END) as Operation
		FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT a
		INNER JOIN TBL_DTS_CONFIG_EVENT b ON b.EventId = a.EventId
		LEFT JOIN TBL_DTS_LOG_MERGELOT m ON m.MergeLotId = a.MergeLotId
		LEFT JOIN TBL_DTS_LOG_SPLITLOT s ON s.SplitLotId = a.SplitLotId
		LEFT JOIN TBL_DTS_LOG_UPDATELOT u ON u.ULogId = a.UpdateLotId
		WHERE EventDateTime between @I_StartDateTime and @I_EndDateTime

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetBinResultType]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 28/05/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To Get BinResult Type

-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 23/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To get LotInfo
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetLotInfo] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT = NULL,
	@I_LotNumber VARCHAR(100) = NULL,
	@O_Success INT = NULL OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)

	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY

			SELECT * FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and LotNumber = @I_LotNumber

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetMotherLotDevices]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 29/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To get devices info for mother lot
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 08/09/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add transaction type for split lot in order to include the scanned device
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetMotherLotDevices] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_tblDevicesId dbo.TDTS_DTS_DEVICE READONLY,
	@I_TransactionType VARCHAR(50),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'GetMotherDevices'
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

			SELECT * INTO #TMPDeviceId FROM @I_tblDevicesId
			
			IF (@I_TransactionType = 'SplitStandard' OR @I_TransactionType = 'SplitNonStandard' OR @I_TransactionType = 'SplitORT')
				BEGIN
					SELECT DTS.LotInfoId, DTS.DeviceId, DTS.AliasId, DTS.SourceSubstrateId, DTS.TargetSubstrateId,
					DTS.SourcePositionId, DTS.TargetPositionId, DTS.FromX, DTS.FromY, DTS.ToX, DTS.ToY,
					BinResult = CASE WHEN BinResult = 'PREV FAILED' THEN 'UNKNOWN' ELSE BinResult END,
					DTS.BinCode, DTS.SAPBarcode, DTS.BinDesc, DTS.LotNumber, DTS.Pick FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS
					INNER JOIN #TMPDeviceId t ON t.DeviceId = DTS.DeviceId
					WHERE DTS.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId
				END
			ELSE
				BEGIN
					SELECT LotInfoId, DeviceId, AliasId, SourceSubstrateId, TargetSubstrateId,
					SourcePositionId, TargetPositionId, FromX, FromY, ToX, ToY,
					BinResult = CASE WHEN BinResult = 'PREV FAILED' THEN 'UNKNOWN' ELSE BinResult END,
					BinCode, SAPBarcode, BinDesc, LotNumber, Pick
					FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
					WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId NOT IN (SELECT * FROM #TMPDeviceId)
				END

			DROP TABLE #TMPDeviceId

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetnUpdateQuantityLotInfo]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 09/09/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To update DTS device quantity to Lotinfo table
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetnUpdateQuantityLotInfo] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_TransactionType VARCHAR(50),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_DeviceQuantity INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'UpdateQuantityLotInfo'
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
			
			IF(@I_TransactionType = 'ValidatePass')
				BEGIN
					SELECT @O_DeviceQuantity = COUNT(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
					WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND BinResult = 'PASS'
				END
			ELSE IF (@I_TransactionType = 'ValidateFail')
				BEGIN
					SELECT @O_DeviceQuantity = COUNT(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
					WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND BinResult = 'FAIL'
				END
			ELSE
				BEGIN
					SELECT @O_DeviceQuantity = COUNT(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
					WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND BinResult != 'PREV FAILED'
				END

			UPDATE TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO
			SET ValidateQuantity = @O_DeviceQuantity
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId
			
		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 06/09/2021
-- Version: 1.0.0.0
-- Description:	Get scanned device list from temp table
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetScannedDevice] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_Operation BIGINT,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	SET @O_Success = 0

	SELECT LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ValidateResult
	FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
	WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation

	RETURN  @O_Success
END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 29/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To get selected devices info
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 08/09/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add transaction type for split lot in order to exclude the scanned device
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 03/11/2021
-- Version		: 3.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add selectedPassDevices for split device in order to exclude the fail and prev failed device
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetSelectedDeviceInfo]
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_tblDevicesId dbo.TDTS_DTS_DEVICE READONLY,
	@I_TransactionType VARCHAR(50),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'GetChildDevices'
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

			SELECT * INTO #TMPDeviceId FROM @I_tblDevicesId

			IF (@I_TransactionType = 'SplitStandard' OR @I_TransactionType = 'SplitNonStandard' OR @I_TransactionType = 'SplitORT')
				BEGIN
					SELECT LotInfoId, DeviceId, AliasId, SourceSubstrateId, TargetSubstrateId,
					SourcePositionId, TargetPositionId, FromX, FromY, ToX, ToY,
					BinResult = CASE WHEN BinResult = 'PREV FAILED' THEN 'UNKNOWN' ELSE BinResult END,
					BinCode, SAPBarcode, BinDesc, LotNumber, Pick
					FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
					WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId NOT IN (SELECT * FROM #TMPDeviceId)
				END
			ELSE IF (@I_TransactionType = 'SelectedPassDevices')
				BEGIN
					SELECT DTS.LotInfoId, DTS.DeviceId, DTS.AliasId, DTS.SourceSubstrateId, DTS.TargetSubstrateId,
					DTS.SourcePositionId, DTS.TargetPositionId, DTS.FromX, DTS.FromY, DTS.ToX, DTS.ToY,
					BinResult = CASE WHEN BinResult = 'PREV FAILED' THEN 'UNKNOWN' ELSE BinResult END,
					DTS.BinCode, DTS.SAPBarcode, DTS.BinDesc, DTS.LotNumber, DTS.Pick FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS
					INNER JOIN #TMPDeviceId t ON t.DeviceId = DTS.DeviceId
					WHERE DTS.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DTS.BinResult NOT IN ('FAIL', 'PREV FAILED')
				END
			ELSE
				BEGIN
					SELECT DTS.LotInfoId, DTS.DeviceId, DTS.AliasId, DTS.SourceSubstrateId, DTS.TargetSubstrateId,
					DTS.SourcePositionId, DTS.TargetPositionId, DTS.FromX, DTS.FromY, DTS.ToX, DTS.ToY,
					BinResult = CASE WHEN BinResult = 'PREV FAILED' THEN 'UNKNOWN' ELSE BinResult END,
					DTS.BinCode, DTS.SAPBarcode, DTS.BinDesc, DTS.LotNumber, DTS.Pick FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS
					INNER JOIN #TMPDeviceId t ON t.DeviceId = DTS.DeviceId
					WHERE DTS.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId
				END

			DROP TABLE #TMPDeviceId

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetValidationResultLogID]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 09/09/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Get Validation log ID
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_GetValidationResultLogID]
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_Operation BIGINT,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_VLogID INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)

	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
	
	SELECT @O_VLogID = VLogId FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
	WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and Operation = @I_Operation

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertAuditLog]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 07/05/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Insert Audit Log
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 06/09/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Add additional event id
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertAuditLog]

	@I_UserId VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@I_EventId BIGINT = NULL,
	@I_TransactionId BIGINT = NULL,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @currDateTime DATETIME
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertAuditLog'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @currDateTime = GETDATE()

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

		--EventId 3 = Split
		--EventId 4 = Merge
		--EventId 5 = Update
		--EventId 6 = BatchUpdate
		--7 = SplitStandard
        --8 = SplitNonStandard
        --9 = SplitORT
        --10 = Validate Pass Device
        --11 = Validate Fail Device
        --12 = Validate Sampling Device
		IF (@I_EventId = 3 OR @I_EventId = 7  OR @I_EventId = 8  OR @I_EventId = 9) 
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime, SplitLotId)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime, @I_TransactionId)
			END
		ELSE IF (@I_EventId = 4)
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime, MergeLotId)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime, @I_TransactionId)
			END
		ELSE IF (@I_EventId = 5 OR @I_EventId = 6)
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime, UpdateLotId)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime, @I_TransactionId)
			END
		ELSE IF (@I_EventId = 10 OR @I_EventId = 11 OR @I_EventId = 12)
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime, ValidateLotId)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime, @I_TransactionId)
			END
		ELSE
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime)
			END

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertAuditLog_bkp20211015]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 07/05/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Insert Audit Log
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertAuditLog_bkp20211015]

	@I_UserId VARCHAR(50) = NULL,
	@I_EventId BIGINT = NULL,
	@I_TransactionId BIGINT = NULL,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @currDateTime DATETIME
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertAuditLog'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @currDateTime = GETDATE()

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

		--EventId 3 = Split
		--EventId 4 = Merge
		--EventId 5 = Update
		--EventId 6 = BatchUpdate
		IF (@I_EventId = 3) 
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime, SplitLotId)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime, @I_TransactionId)
			END
		ELSE IF (@I_EventId = 4)
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime, MergeLotId)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime, @I_TransactionId)
			END
		ELSE IF (@I_EventId = 5 OR @I_EventId = 6)
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime, UpdateLotId)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime, @I_TransactionId)
			END
		ELSE
			BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_AUDIT
			(UserId, EventId, EventDateTime)
			VALUES
			(@I_UserId, @I_EventId, @currDateTime)
			END

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertBatchUpdateLot]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 2021-06-16
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To Insert Batch Update Lot Info
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 2022-02-21
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Added Transaction type To Insert Batch Update FL Log
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertBatchUpdateLot]
	@I_tblBUpdateDeviceInfo dbo.TDTS_DTS_DEVICE READONLY,
	@I_LotNumber VARCHAR(100),
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_Operation VARCHAR(50),
	@I_SourceSubstrateId VARCHAR(100),
	@I_TargetSubstrateId VARCHAR(100),
	@I_BinResult VARCHAR(100),
	@I_BinCode VARCHAR(100),
	@I_BinDesc VARCHAR(100),
	@O_UpdateLotLogId BIGINT OUTPUT,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @V_CurrDateTime DATETIME
	DECLARE @BinResultName VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertBatchUpdateLotInfo'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @V_CurrDateTime = GETDATE()

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		
				SELECT * INTO #TMPDETROSBatchUpdateDTSInfo FROM @I_tblBUpdateDeviceInfo

				SELECT @BinResultName = BinResultName FROM TBL_DTS_CONFIG_BINRESULT
				WHERE BinResultId = @I_BinResult

						INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_UPDATELOT(UpdateLotNumber, Operation, DeviceId, AliasId,
						SourceSubstrateId, TargetSubstrateId, SourcePositionId, TargetPositionId, FromX, FromY, ToX
						, ToY, BinResult, BinCode, LotInfoId, UpdateDateTime, IsBatchUpdate, BinDesc)
						SELECT 
						@I_LotNumber,
						@I_Operation,
						DI.DeviceId,
						'',
						SourceSubstrateId = CASE WHEN @I_SourceSubstrateId IS NOT NULL THEN @I_SourceSubstrateId ELSE SourceSubstrateId END,
						TargetSubstrateId = CASE WHEN @I_TargetSubstrateId IS NOT NULL THEN @I_TargetSubstrateId ELSE TargetSubstrateId END,
						'',
						'',
						'',
						'',
						'',
						'',
						BinResult = CASE WHEN @BinResultName != '' THEN @BinResultName ELSE BinResult END,
						BinCode = CASE WHEN @I_BinCode IS NOT NULL THEN @I_BinCode ELSE BinCode END,
						@I_LotInfoId,
						@V_CurrDateTime,
						1,
						BinDesc = CASE WHEN @I_BinDesc IS NOT NULL THEN @I_BinDesc ELSE BinDesc END
						FROM #TMPDETROSBatchUpdateDTSInfo DI
						INNER JOIN dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS ON  DTS.DeviceId = DI.DeviceId
						WHERE DTS.LotNumber = @I_LotNumber and DTS.LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId
				
				SELECT @O_UpdateLotLogId = IDENT_CURRENT('dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_UPDATELOT')

				DROP TABLE #TMPDETROSBatchUpdateDTSInfo

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertDeviceInfo]

	@I_tblDTSInfoValue dbo.TDTS_DTS_DATA READONLY,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertDeviceInfo'
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
			
			SELECT * INTO #TMPDETROSDTSInfo FROM @I_tblDTSInfoValue
			
			INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS(LotInfoId,DeviceId,AliasId,SourceSubstrateId,TargetSubstrateId,SourcePositionId,TargetPositionId,FromX,FromY,ToX
			,ToY,BinResult,BinCode,BinDesc,LotNumber,Pick)
			SELECT	DI.LotInfoId,
			DI.DeviceId, DI.AliasId, DI.SourceSubstrateId, DI.TargetSubstrateId, DI.SourcePositionId, DI.TargetPositionId, DI.FromX, DI.FromY, DI.ToX
			, DI.ToY, DI.BinResult, DI.BinCode, DI.BinDesc, DI.LotNumber, DI.Pick
			FROM  #TMPDETROSDTSInfo DI

			DROP TABLE #TMPDETROSDTSInfo

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertMergeLot]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 23/04/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To Insert MergeLot data
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 11/08/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: To add in additional 3 child lot number
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertMergeLot] 
	@I_MotherLotNumber VARCHAR(50) NULL,
	@I_ChildLotNumber VARCHAR(50) NULL,
	@I_ChildLotNumber2 VARCHAR(50) NULL,
	@I_ChildLotNumber3 VARCHAR(50) NULL,
	@I_ChildLotNumber4 VARCHAR(50) NULL,
	@I_Operation VARCHAR(50) NULL,
	@O_MergeId BIGINT OUTPUT,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @currentRecord INT,
	@currDate DATETIME

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @CurrentRecord = 0
	SET @currDate = GETDATE()
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertMergeLot'

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

			SELECT @currentRecord=COUNT(MergeLotId) FROM  dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_MERGELOT
			WHERE MotherLotId = @I_MotherLotNumber and ChildLotId = @I_ChildLotNumber

			IF (@currentRecord = 0)
				BEGIN

					INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_MERGELOT
					(MotherLotId, ChildLotId, MergeDateTime, Operation,
					ChildLotId2, ChildLotId3, ChildLotId4)
					VALUES
					(@I_MotherLotNumber, @I_ChildLotNumber, @currDate, @I_Operation,
					@I_ChildLotNumber2, @I_ChildLotNumber3, @I_ChildLotNumber4)

					SELECT @O_MergeId = IDENT_CURRENT('dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_MERGELOT')
				END
			ELSE
				BEGIN

					UPDATE dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_MERGELOT
					SET MergeDateTime = @currDate
					where MotherLotId = @I_MotherLotNumber and ChildLotId = @I_ChildLotNumber

					SELECT @O_MergeId = IDENT_CURRENT('dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_MERGELOT')
				END

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertUpdateLot]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 2021-06-16
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: To Insert Update Lot Info
-- =============================================
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 2022-02-21
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: Added In Transaction type to handle FL update log
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertUpdateLot]
	@I_Operation VARCHAR(50),
	@I_TblUpdateDTSInfoValue dbo.TDTS_DTS_DATA READONLY,
	@O_UpdateEditLotLogId BIGINT OUTPUT,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @V_CurrDateTime DATETIME

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertUpdateLotInfo'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @V_CurrDateTime = GETDATE()

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

				SELECT t.LotInfoId, t.DeviceId, t.AliasId, t.SourceSubstrateId, t.TargetSubstrateId, t.SourcePositionId,
				t.TargetPositionId, t.FromX, t.FromY, t.ToX, t.ToY, b.BinResultName as BinResult, t.BinCode, t.BinDesc, t.LotNumber, t.Pick 
				INTO #TMPDETROSUpdateEditDTSInfo FROM @I_TblUpdateDTSInfoValue t
				inner join TBL_DTS_CONFIG_BINRESULT b on b.BinResultId = CAST(t.BinResult as bigint)

				INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_UPDATELOT(UpdateLotNumber, Operation, DeviceId, AliasId,
				SourceSubstrateId, TargetSubstrateId, SourcePositionId, TargetPositionId, FromX, FromY, ToX
				, ToY, BinResult, BinCode, LotInfoId, UpdateDateTime, IsBatchUpdate, BinDesc)
				SELECT	DI.LotNumber, @I_Operation, DI.DeviceId, DI.AliasId, DI.SourceSubstrateId, 
				DI.TargetSubstrateId, DI.SourcePositionId, DI.TargetPositionId, DI.FromX, DI.FromY, DI.ToX
				, DI.ToY, 
				CASE WHEN DI.BinResult != '' THEN DI.BinResult ELSE DTS.BinResult END,
				DI.BinCode, DI.LotInfoId, @V_CurrDateTime, 0, DI.BinDesc
				FROM  #TMPDETROSUpdateEditDTSInfo DI
				INNER JOIN dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS ON DTS.DeviceId = DI.DeviceId
				WHERE DTS.LotNumber = DI.LotNumber and DTS.LotInfoId = DI.LotInfoId

				DROP TABLE #TMPDETROSUpdateEditDTSInfo

			SELECT @O_UpdateEditLotLogId = IDENT_CURRENT('dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_UPDATELOT')

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertUserManagement]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 08/03/2022
-- Description:	To insert user management log
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertUserManagement] 
	@Tbl_UserTrans TDTS_DTS_User READONLY,
	@I_UserId VARCHAR(250),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_UserManageLogId BIGINT OUTPUT,
	@O_ErrTxt VARCHAR(250) OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @V_CurrDateTime DATETIME

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertUserManagement'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @V_CurrDateTime = GETDATE()

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		
		SELECT * INTO TMPUserTrans FROM @Tbl_UserTrans

		INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_USERMANAGEMENT(UpdateBy, UpdatedUser, UpdatedRole, UpdateOn)
		SELECT	
		@I_UserId, tmp.UserId, tmp.RoleId, @V_CurrDateTime
		FROM  TMPUserTrans tmp

		DROP TABLE TMPUserTrans

		SELECT @O_UserManageLogId = IDENT_CURRENT('dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_USERMANAGEMENT')


		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		SET @O_ErrTxt = @ERR_MSG
	END CATCH
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertValidationResult]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 06/09/2021
-- Version: 1.0.0.0
-- Description:	Validate the scanned device list and insert validation result
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_InsertValidationResult] 
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_Operation BIGINT,
	@I_ValidationType VARCHAR(50),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_ValidationResult VARCHAR(10) OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @ConditionCount INT, @CurrDateTime DATETIME, @DifBinDescCount INT
	DECLARE @QuantityCheck INT, @ScannedQuantity INT, @ValidateQuantity INT, @CurrRecordCount INT

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'InsertValidationResult'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @ConditionCount = 0
	SET @DifBinDescCount = 0
	SET @QuantityCheck = 0
	SET @CurrRecordCount = 0
	SET @CurrDateTime = GETDATE()

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		
		SELECT @ValidateQuantity = ValidateQuantity FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO
		WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and Operation = @I_Operation

		SELECT @CurrRecordCount = COUNT(VLogId) FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
		WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and Operation = @I_Operation

		IF (@I_ValidationType = 'ValidateFail')
		BEGIN
			SELECT @ConditionCount = Count(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND (BinResult = 'PASS' OR BinDesc IS NULL)

			--SELECT @DifBinDescCount = Count (DISTINCT BinDesc) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			--WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND BinResult = 'FAIL'

			SELECT @ScannedQuantity = Count (DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation

			IF (@ScannedQuantity != @ValidateQuantity)
			BEGIN
				SET @QuantityCheck = 1
			END

		END
		ELSE IF (@I_ValidationType = 'SplitNonStandard')
		BEGIN
			SELECT @ConditionCount = Count(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND (BinResult = 'FAIL' OR BinDesc IS NULL)

			SELECT @DifBinDescCount = Count (DISTINCT BinDesc) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND BinResult = 'PASS'

			SELECT @ScannedQuantity = Count (DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation

			IF (@ScannedQuantity >= @ValidateQuantity)
			BEGIN
				SET @QuantityCheck = 1
			END
		END
		ELSE IF (@I_ValidationType = 'ValidateSampling')
		BEGIN
			SELECT @ConditionCount = Count(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND (BinResult = 'FAIL' OR BinDesc IS NULL)

			SELECT @DifBinDescCount = Count (DISTINCT BinDesc) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND BinResult = 'PASS'

			SELECT @ScannedQuantity = Count (DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation

			IF (@ScannedQuantity > @ValidateQuantity)
			BEGIN
				SET @QuantityCheck = 1
			END
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN
			SELECT @ConditionCount = Count(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND (BinResult = 'FAIL' OR BinDesc IS NULL)

			SELECT @DifBinDescCount = Count (DISTINCT BinDesc) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND BinResult = 'PASS'

			SELECT @ScannedQuantity = Count (DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation

			IF (@ScannedQuantity != @ValidateQuantity)
			BEGIN
				SET @QuantityCheck = 1
			END
		END
		
		IF (@CurrRecordCount > 0)
			BEGIN
				IF (@QuantityCheck > 0)
					BEGIN 
						SET @O_ValidationResult = 'FAIL Q'
						UPDATE dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
						SET ValidationResult = 'FAIL', ValidateDateTime = @CurrDateTime
						WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation
					END
				ELSE IF (@DifBinDescCount > 1)
					BEGIN
						SET @O_ValidationResult = 'FAIL B'
						UPDATE dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
						SET ValidationResult = 'FAIL', ValidateDateTime = @CurrDateTime
						WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation
					END
				ELSE IF (@ConditionCount > 0)
					BEGIN
						SET @O_ValidationResult = 'FAIL F'
						UPDATE dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
						SET ValidationResult = 'FAIL', ValidateDateTime = @CurrDateTime
						WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation
					END
				ELSE
					BEGIN
						SET @O_ValidationResult = 'PASS'
						UPDATE dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
						SET ValidationResult = 'PASS', ValidateDateTime = @CurrDateTime
						WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation
					END
			END
		ELSE
			BEGIN
				IF (@QuantityCheck > 0)
					BEGIN 
				SET @O_ValidationResult = 'FAIL Q'
				INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
				(LotInfoId, ValidationResult, Operation, ValidateDateTime)
				VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, 'FAIL', @I_Operation, @CurrDateTime)
			END
				ELSE IF (@DifBinDescCount > 1)
					BEGIN
				SET @O_ValidationResult = 'FAIL B'
				INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
				(LotInfoId, ValidationResult, Operation, ValidateDateTime)
				VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, 'FAIL', @I_Operation, @CurrDateTime)
			END
				ELSE IF (@ConditionCount > 0)
					BEGIN
				SET @O_ValidationResult = 'FAIL F'
				INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
				(LotInfoId, ValidationResult, Operation, ValidateDateTime)
				VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, 'FAIL', @I_Operation, @CurrDateTime)
			END
				ELSE
					BEGIN
				SET @O_ValidationResult = 'PASS'
				INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_VALIDATIONRESULT
				(LotInfoId, ValidationResult, Operation, ValidateDateTime)
				VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, 'PASS', @I_Operation, @CurrDateTime)
			END
			END
		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_ModifyUserInfo]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 08/03/2022
-- Description:	Change Role and delete user
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_ModifyUserInfo]
	@Tbl_UpdateUsers TDTS_DTS_USER READONLY,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_ErrTxt VARCHAR(250) OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @V_UserCount INT

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'ModifyUserInfo'
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @V_UserCount = 0
	SET @O_ErrTxt = ''

		BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		
		SELECT * INTO TMPUserList FROM @Tbl_UpdateUsers
		SELECT * INTO TMPUserList1 FROM @Tbl_UpdateUsers

		SELECT @V_UserCount = COUNT(u.UserId) FROM TBL_DTS_USER u
		INNER JOIN TMPUserList tmp ON tmp.UserId = u.UserId
		WHERE u.UserId = tmp.UserId

		IF (@V_UserCount = 0)
		BEGIN
			SET @O_Success = 1
			SET @O_ErrTxt = 'User not found'
		END
		ELSE 
		BEGIN
			UPDATE TBL_DTS_USER
			SET
			RoleId = tmp1.RoleId
			FROM TBL_DTS_USER u1
			INNER JOIN TMPUserList1 tmp1 ON tmp1.UserId = u1.UserId
			WHERE u1.UserId = tmp1.UserId
		END

		DROP TABLE TMPUserList
		DROP TABLE TMPUserList1

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		SET @O_ErrTxt = @ERR_MSG
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_UpdateDeviceInfo]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 06/05/2021
-- Version		: 1.0.0.0
-- Description	: Update Device Info
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_UpdateDeviceInfo]
(
	@I_tblDTSInfoValue dbo.TDTS_DTS_DATA READONLY,
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT
)
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	
	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'UpdateDeviceInfo'
	SET @O_Success = 0

	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

			SELECT t.LotInfoId, t.DeviceId, t.AliasId, t.SourceSubstrateId, t.TargetSubstrateId, t.SourcePositionId,
			t.TargetPositionId, t.FromX, t.FromY, t.ToX, t.ToY, b.BinResultName as BinResult, t.BinCode, t.BinDesc, t.LotNumber, t.Pick 
			INTO #TMPUpdatedDETROSDTSInfo FROM @I_tblDTSInfoValue t
			inner join TBL_DTS_CONFIG_BINRESULT b on b.BinResultId = CAST(t.BinResult as bigint)

			UPDATE TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
			SET AliasId=DI.AliasId,
			SourceSubstrateId=DI.SourceSubstrateId,
			TargetSubstrateId=DI.TargetSubstrateId,
			SourcePositionId=DI.SourcePositionId,
			TargetPositionId=DI.TargetPositionId,
			FromX=DI.FromX,
			FromY=DI.FromY,
			ToX=DI.ToX,
			ToY=DI.ToY, 
			BinResult = CASE WHEN DI.BinResult != '' THEN DI.BinResult ELSE DTS.BinResult END,
			BinCode=DI.BinCode,
			BinDesc=DI.BinDesc,
			Pick=DI.Pick
			FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS DTS
			INNER JOIN #TMPUpdatedDETROSDTSInfo DI ON  DI.DeviceId = DTS.DeviceId
			WHERE DTS.LotNumber = DI.LotNumber and DTS.LotInfoId = DI.LotInfoId
			
			DROP TABLE #TMPUpdatedDETROSDTSInfo	
		
		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_ValidateLogin]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author: Jackson
-- Create date: 08/03/2022
-- Description:	Validate login
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_ValidateLogin] 
	@I_UserName VARCHAR(50),
	@I_Password VARCHAR(250),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_ErrTxt VARCHAR(250) OUTPUT,
	@O_Role VARCHAR(50) OUTPUT
AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @UserCount INT, @PassCount INT
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @O_ErrTxt = ''

	SELECT @UserCount = COUNT(UserId) FROM TBL_DTS_USER
	WHERE UserId = @I_UserName AND Active = 1

	SELECT @PassCount = COUNT(UserId) FROM TBL_DTS_USER
	WHERE UserId = @I_UserName AND Password = @I_Password AND Active = 1

	IF (@UserCount = 0)
		BEGIN
			SET @O_Success = 1
			SET @O_ErrTxt = 'User not found!'
		END
	ELSE IF (@PassCount = 0)
		BEGIN
			SET @O_Success = 2
			SET @O_ErrTxt = 'Password not match!'
		END
	ELSE IF (@UserCount > 0 AND @PassCount > 0)
		BEGIN

			SELECT @O_Role = r.RoleName
			FROM TBL_DTS_USER u
			INNER JOIN TBL_DTS_CONFIG_ROLES r ON r.RoleId = u.RoleId
			WHERE u.UserId = @I_UserName AND u.Password = @I_Password AND u.Active = 1

		END
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PR_DTS_ValidateScannedDevice]    Script Date: 3/18/2022 1:08:00 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
-- =============================================
-- Author		: Jackson
-- Create date	: 03/09/2021
-- Version		: 2.0.0.0
-- Description	: To validate the scanned device id with DTS table and insert into temp table
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[PR_DTS_ValidateScannedDevice] 
	@I_DeviceId VARCHAR(50),
	@I_LotInfoId BIGINT,
	@I_Operation BIGINT,
	@I_TransactionType VARCHAR(50),
	@O_Success INT OUTPUT,
	@O_Result INT OUTPUT

AS
BEGIN
	DECLARE @ERR_NUM INT, @ERR_MSG NVARCHAR(4000)
	DECLARE @TRANS_NAME VARCHAR(50)
	DECLARE @RecordCount INT, @DupCount INT, @CurrCount INT
	DECLARE @ScannedBinDesc VARCHAR(50), @PackageCount INT, @BinDesc VARCHAR(50), @ScannedTimeStamp DATETIME
	DECLARE @BinResult VARCHAR(50)

	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	SET @O_Success = 0
	SET @O_Result = 0
	SET @RecordCount = 0
	SET @DupCount = 0
	SET @CurrCount = 0
	SET @TRANS_NAME = 'ValidateScannedDevice'
    
	BEGIN TRY
		BEGIN TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

			SELECT LotInfoId,DeviceId,BinResult,BinCode,BinDesc into #TMPScannedDevice FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO_DTS
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId

			SELECT @RecordCount =  COUNT(DeviceId) FROM #TMPScannedDevice

			SELECT @DupCount = COUNT(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and DeviceId = @I_DeviceId

			SELECT @CurrCount = COUNT(DeviceId) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and Operation = @I_Operation

			SELECT @PackageCount = ValidateQuantity FROM TBL_DTS_LOG_LOTINFO
			WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId and Operation = @I_Operation

			IF (@I_TransactionType = 'SplitNonStandard')
				BEGIN
					-- Check Current count with Package count
					IF (@CurrCount < (@PackageCount - 1)) 
						BEGIN
						-- Check whether the device belong to the lot or not
							IF(@RecordCount = 0)
								BEGIN
								-- Check whether the device been existed in the temp table or not
									IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										-- The scanned device is not belong to the lot!
										SET @O_Result = 2

										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation, ValidateResult)
										VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation, @O_Result)
									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										--The scanned device is already been scanned previously! Please verify!
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
								END
							ELSE
						-- The device belong to the lot
								BEGIN
								-- Check whether the device been existed in the temp table or not
									IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ValidateResult)
										SELECT DS.LotInfoId, DS.DeviceId, DS.BinResult, DS.BinCode, DS.BinDesc, @I_Operation, @O_Result
										FROM #TMPScannedDevice DS

										SELECT @BinResult= BinResult FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

										IF (@BinResult = 'FAIL' OR @BinResult = 'PREV FAILED')
										BEGIN
											--The scanned device is FAIL device!
											SET @O_Result = 1

											UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
											SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
											WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation
										END
										ELSE IF (@BinResult = 'PASS')
											BEGIN
												--SELECT @DifBinDescCount = Count (DISTINCT BinDesc) FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												--WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND BinResult = 'PASS'

												SELECT DISTINCT TOP(1) @BinDesc = BinDesc, @ScannedTimeStamp = ScannedTimeStamp FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND BinResult = 'PASS'
												ORDER BY ScannedTimeStamp ASC

												SELECT @ScannedBinDesc = BinDesc FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

												IF (@ScannedBinDesc <> @BinDesc)
													BEGIN
														--The scanned device is different bin!
														SET @O_Result = 5

															UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
															SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
															WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation
													END
											END
									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
								END
						END
					ELSE
						BEGIN
							IF(@RecordCount = 0)
								BEGIN
									IF (@DupCount = 0)
										BEGIN
											--INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
											--(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation)
											--VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation)

											SET @O_Result = 4

											INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
											(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation, ValidateResult)
											VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation, @O_Result)

										END
									ELSE
										BEGIN
											SET @O_Result = 3
										END
								END
							ELSE
								BEGIN
									IF (@DupCount = 0)
										BEGIN
											--INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
											--(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation)
											--SELECT DS.LotInfoId, DS.DeviceId, DS.BinResult, DS.BinCode, DS.BinDesc, @I_Operation
											--FROM #TMPScannedDevice DS

											--SELECT @BinResult= BinResult FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
											--WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

											--IF (@BinResult = 'FAIL')
											--	BEGIN
											--		SET @O_Result = 4
											--	END

											SET @O_Result = 4

										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ValidateResult)
										SELECT DS.LotInfoId, DS.DeviceId, DS.BinResult, DS.BinCode, DS.BinDesc, @I_Operation, @O_Result
										FROM #TMPScannedDevice DS

										SELECT @BinResult= BinResult FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

										IF (@BinResult = 'FAIL' OR @BinResult = 'PREV FAILED')
											BEGIN
												SET @O_Result = 4

												UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
												WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

											END
										END
									ELSE
										BEGIN
											SET @O_Result = 3
										END
								END
						END
				END
			ELSE IF (@I_TransactionType = 'ValidateFail')
				BEGIN
					IF(@CurrCount < @PackageCount)
					BEGIN
						IF(@RecordCount = 0)
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										--INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										--(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation)
										--VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation)

										SET @O_Result = 2
										
										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation, ValidateResult)
										VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation, @O_Result)

									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
							END
						ELSE
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ValidateResult)
										SELECT DS.LotInfoId, DS.DeviceId, DS.BinResult, DS.BinCode, DS.BinDesc, @I_Operation, @O_Result
										FROM #TMPScannedDevice DS

										SELECT @BinResult= BinResult FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

										IF (@BinResult = 'PASS')
											BEGIN
												SET @O_Result = 1

												UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
												WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

											END
									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
							END
					END
				ELSE
					BEGIN
						IF(@RecordCount = 0)
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										--INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										--(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation)
										--VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation)

										SET @O_Result = 4

										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation, ValidateResult)
										VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation, @O_Result)

									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
							END
						ELSE
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ValidateResult)
										SELECT DS.LotInfoId, DS.DeviceId, DS.BinResult, DS.BinCode, DS.BinDesc, @I_Operation, @O_Result
										FROM #TMPScannedDevice DS

										SELECT @BinResult= BinResult FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

										IF (@BinResult = 'PASS')
											BEGIN
												SET @O_Result = 4

												UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
												WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

											END

										SET @O_Result = 4

										UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
										WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
							END
					END
				END
			ELSE
				BEGIN
					IF(@CurrCount < @PackageCount)
					BEGIN
						IF(@RecordCount = 0)
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										--INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										--(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation)
										--		VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation)

											SET @O_Result = 2

											INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
											(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation, ValidateResult)
											VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation, @O_Result)

									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
							END
						ELSE
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
											BEGIN
												INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ValidateResult)
												SELECT DS.LotInfoId, DS.DeviceId, DS.BinResult, DS.BinCode, DS.BinDesc, @I_Operation, @O_Result
												FROM #TMPScannedDevice DS

												SELECT @BinResult= BinResult FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

												IF (@BinResult = 'FAIL' OR @BinResult = 'PREV FAILED')
												BEGIN
													SET @O_Result = 1

													UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
													SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
													WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

												END
												ELSE IF (@BinResult = 'PASS')
													BEGIN
														SELECT DISTINCT TOP(1) @BinDesc = BinDesc, @ScannedTimeStamp = ScannedTimeStamp FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
														WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND Operation = @I_Operation AND BinResult = 'PASS'
														ORDER BY ScannedTimeStamp ASC

														SELECT @ScannedBinDesc = BinDesc FROM TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
														WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

														IF (@ScannedBinDesc <> @BinDesc)
														BEGIN
															SET @O_Result = 5

															UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
															SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
															WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

														END
													END
											END
										ELSE
											BEGIN
												SET @O_Result = 3
											END
							END
					END
				ELSE
					BEGIN
						IF(@RecordCount = 0)
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										--INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										--(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation)
										--VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation)

										SET @O_Result = 4

										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, Operation, ValidateResult)
										VALUES (@I_LotInfoId, @I_DeviceId, @I_Operation, @O_Result)

									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
							END
						ELSE
							BEGIN
								IF (@DupCount = 0)
									BEGIN
										INSERT INTO dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										(LotInfoId, DeviceId, BinResult, BinCode, BinDesc, Operation, ValidateResult)
										SELECT DS.LotInfoId, DS.DeviceId, DS.BinResult, DS.BinCode, DS.BinDesc, @I_Operation, @O_Result
										FROM #TMPScannedDevice DS

										SELECT @BinResult= BinResult FROM dbo.TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

										IF (@BinResult = 'FAIL' OR @BinResult = 'PREV FAILED')
											BEGIN
												SET @O_Result = 4
												
												UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
												SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
												WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

											END

										SET @O_Result = 4

										UPDATE TBL_DTS_TEMP_SCANDEVICEINFO
										SET ValidateResult = @O_Result
										WHERE LotInfoId = @I_LotInfoId AND DeviceId = @I_DeviceId AND Operation = @I_Operation

									END
								ELSE
									BEGIN
										SET @O_Result = 3
									END
							END
					END
				END
			
			DROP TABLE #TMPScannedDevice

		COMMIT TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME

	END TRY
	BEGIN CATCH
		SET @O_Success = -1
		SELECT @ERR_NUM = ERROR_NUMBER(), @ERR_MSG = ERROR_MESSAGE()
		ROLLBACK TRANSACTION @TRANS_NAME
		RAISERROR (@ERR_MSG, 16, 1, @ERR_NUM)
		RETURN @O_Success
	END CATCH
END
GO
USE [master]
GO
ALTER DATABASE [DTSDB] SET  READ_WRITE 
GO
